				}
			}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_one_language_one_religion_one_nation }
				add_stability = 0.002
			}
			FROM = {
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_temp_state_population = state_population }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_temp_state_population = -5 }
				add_manpower = TUR_temp_state_population
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level < 2 }

						TUR_add_armenian_effect = yes
					}

						TUR_add_albanian_effect = yes
					}

						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
							add_core_of = ROOT
						}
						set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor = 0 }
						set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies = 0 }
						set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0 }
						set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_factories = 0 }
						set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor = 0 }
						set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_war_support_factor = 0 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = GRE }
						remove_core_of = GRE
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = PON }
						remove_core_of = PON
					}
				}
				else = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_level_down
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_factories < 0 } }
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_factories_down
						add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_factories = 0.05 }
					}
					if = {

						add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies = -0.1 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor < 0 } }
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_recruitable_population_down
						add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor = 0.05 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor > 0 } }
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_construction_speed_down
						add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.02 }
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_stability_war_support_down
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor < 0 } }
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_stability_down
						add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_stability_factor = 0.002 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_war_support_factor < 0 } }
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_war_support_down
						add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_war_support_factor = 0.001 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level = -1 }
				set_state_flag = TUR_greek_breakdown_of_economic_infrastructure
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_greek_breakdown_of_economic_infrastructure } }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_breakdown_of_economic_infrastructure } } }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_breakdown_of_economic_infrastructure days = 780 }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ottoman.99 days = 365 random_days = 730 }
			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes

				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {

					NOT = {

					}
				}
			}
		}

	TUR_promote_ittihadist_officers = {
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_army_support_ittihadist
		cost = 30
		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_depoliticize_the_army
				has_completed_focus = TUR_promote_young_officers
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_not_ittihadist_loyalty_tt_loyal
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_loyalty < 5 }
			}
			command_power > 15
		}
		activation = { always = no }
		remove_effect = {
			TUR_increase_ittihadist_loyalty = yes
			TUR_decrease_itilafist_loyalty = yes
			add_command_power = -15
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_action_army_coup }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_action_army_coup days = 50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte days = 50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_nationalist_retaliation }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_nationalist_retaliation days = 50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TUR_army_civilian_struggle } }
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = TUR_army_civilian_struggle
					value = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 35

	TUR_arrest_ittihadist_officers = {
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_arrest_ittihadist
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_30
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 29.99 }
		visible = { has_completed_focus = TUR_depoliticize_the_army }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_not_ittihadist_power_tt_minimal
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power > 1 }
			}
		}
		activation = { always = no }
		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -30 }
			TUR_decrease_ittihadist_loyalty = yes
			TUR_decrease_ittihadist_power = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_unit_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
						}
					}
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
						}
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_command_power = -30
				army_experience = -30
				add_war_support = -0.02
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_action_army_coup }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_action_army_coup days = -10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte days = -10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_nationalist_retaliation }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_nationalist_retaliation days = -10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TUR_army_civilian_struggle } }
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = TUR_army_civilian_struggle
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 35

TUR_economy_decision = {
	TUR_dissolve_the_debt_council = {
		icon = gre_investment_decisions
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 300
		visible = { NOT = { has_focus_tree = kostantiniyye_focus_tree } }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_dissolve_the_debt_council_tooltip

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = ENG
					tag = AUH
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = { NOT = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		available = {
			FROM = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = ROOT
					value > 0
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
				has_country_flag = has_active_purchase_contract
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = TUR_OPDA_trigger_tooltip
					NOT = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				TUR_has_land_connection = yes
				enemies_naval_strength_ratio < 3
			}
		}
		cost = 10
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 30
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				}
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					tag = ENG
					AND = {
						tag = GER
						TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_new_weapon_contracts }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = AUH
						TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_new_weapon_contracts }
					}
				}
			}
			has_variable = opda_consumer_goods
			NOT = {
				has_focus_tree = kostantiniyye_focus_tree
				has_focus_tree = turkey_focus_tree
				has_completed_focus = TUR_domestic_weapon_companies
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = has_active_purchase_contract
				days = 30
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = GER
					}
					ROOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_german_ottoman_arms_deal }
				}
				TUR_add_debt_2_FROM = yes
			}
			else = {
				TUR_add_debt_3_FROM = yes
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = {
				flag = has_active_purchase_contract
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_import_dependency }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 200
					producer = FROM
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 150
					producer = FROM
				}
			}
			TUR_foreign_weapon_improvement = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					num_of_civilian_factories < 5
					has_equipment = {
						artillery_equipment > 100
					}
					has_idea = TUR_dependence_on_imported_weapons_4
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 10
			}
		}
